<script>
//<![CDATA[

  $j(document).ready(function() {
    var container = $j("#tos_prompt");
    var outer = $j("#outer");
    var button = $j("#accept_tos");

    setTimeout(showTOSPrompt, 1500);

    function showTOSPrompt() {
      $j.when(container.fadeIn(500)).done(function() {
        outer.addClass("hidden").attr("aria-hidden", "true");
      });

      $j("#tos_agree").on("click", function() {
        button.attr("disabled", !this.checked);
        if (this.checked) {
          button.on("click", function() {
            acceptTOS();
            outer.removeClass("hidden").removeAttr("aria-hidden");
            $j.when(container.fadeOut(500)).done(function() {
              container.remove();
            });
          });
        };
      }).change();
    };
  });

//]]]]><![CDATA[>
</script>

  <!--summary-->
    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>Harry's been kept in the dark for so long, about so many things. After the third task of the Tri-wizard tournament quite a few secrets come to light and darkness seems like home to him. He makes new friends while trying to keep the old and learns magic he'd never knew existed.</p>
    </blockquote>

    <ul class="series">
        <li>
          Part <strong>1</strong> of <a href="/series/1801384">Heirs of Magic</a>
        </li>
    </ul>

    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>She lived through the war, but did she actually survive it? She didn't recognize the girl who looked back at her in the mirror, with sunken eyes and protruding ribs covered in scars. This wasn‚Äôt Hermione Granger. She died alongside Lavender, Fred, Sirius, Remus... Her name wasn‚Äôt up on any walls in memoriam, but she felt like a casualty nonetheless. </p><p>*****</p><p>When Hermione can't seem to get past the trauma of the war and all that happened to her, she's convinced to get help for her mental health issues. Unfortunately, the Wizarding World has none... yet.</p>

    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>
  <strong>** NOT COMPLETED YET **</strong>
</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>A Golden Girl missing.<br>A Slytherin Prince trapped.<br>An Order holding secrets.<br>And a Dark Lord ruling.<br><br><strong>Warning:</strong> Dark AU (not dark main character) with deep discussions of trauma caused by physical, emotional, and sexual abuse.<br><br>This fic starts out in the midst of the darkness, and shows the trauma, and healing journeys of each character as they fight to keep as much of themselves as possible, in a world trying to take it all.</p><p>(The rape is <strong>not</strong> between Draco and Hermione)</p>
    </blockquote>

  <!--summary-->
    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>Lucretia Black never considered herself lucky. She thought it woefully ironic that her parents had chosen a name meaning luck for their daughter, considering the fate that soon befell them. Having spent nearly her whole life living a tenuous lie, she‚Äôs surrounded herself with walls, boundaries for her own protection. She‚Äôs been wronged before, after all, by people like Julian Rosier, whom she once considered friends. Can she let down her defenses for love? Or will her pride and his prejudice lead to the downfall of them both?</p>
    </blockquote>

    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>Anne Potter was sent back in time in hopes of fixing everything after the Order lost the Second Wizarding War and hoping to pay back everything Harry had ever done for her by giving him a normal childhood.</p>
<p>She learns, however, that even after everything she done and went through, she still deserves a happy ending, even if she had to fight for it.</p>
    </blockquote>

    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>One year has passed since Lyra (formerly Bellatrix) Black traveled thirty years into an alternate future. Unfortunately, this means she's expected to go back to boring Hogwarts for more boring normal people stuff. Except, there is that Tournament thing. And Angel Black. And her muggleborn girlfriend. And maybe an international incident or two... Never mind, should be fun.</p>

    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>What if the Triwizard Tournament had a Slytherin champion instead of Cedric Diggory?</p><p>On the surface, Ophelia Warrington is the embodiment of the ideal teenage witch: attractive, intelligent, and well-respected. To her closest friends, she's the antithesis of the stereotypical Slytherin pureblood. Being the sister of a champion and Draco Malfoy's best friend is already a struggle, what's the worse that can happen?</p><p>gof-??</p><p>~</p><p>"Hagrid says you're one of his best students."</p><p>"You talk to Hagrid about me?"</p><p>"I‚Äîum, it's not what you think."</p><p>"Potter, how many times do I have to tell you I'm joking."</p><p>"I don't know, you seem pretty serious most of the time."</p><p>"Ah, you're not wrong. But maybe that's just what I want everyone to think."</p><p>~</p><p>also on ff.net and wattpad under the same username</p>

  <!--summary-->
    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>Harry Potter is twice-orphaned by the time he's nine years old. When his Aunt Petunia and Uncle Vernon die in a car crash before his ninth birthday, he's sent with his cousin Dudley to live with Aunt Marge. Unfortunately, Aunt Marge drops him off at what she thinks is an orphanage, leaving Harry in the care of children's services. </p><p>A year later, Remus Lupin comes looking for his best friend's son, to check on his welfare. When he finds Harry missing, he asks for his father's help in getting Harry to safety and family. As Remus, Lyall, and Harry navigate their new family dynamics, they are challenged by all parts of the wizarding world, and by the mysterious events that follow with Harry's years at Hogwarts. Chapters will alternate between Harry POV and Remus POV, unless otherwise stated.</p><p>Part 1: Covers 1990-1994, including the year before Harry's first year at Hogwarts through the end of canon's Prisoner of Azkaban.</p><p>Canon compliant relationships. </p><p>*Updates on Sundays and Wednesdays*</p>
    </blockquote>

    <h6 class="landmark heading">Series</h6>
    <ul class="series">
        <li>
          Part <strong>1</strong> of <a href="/series/2758126">Harry and the Lupins</a>
        </li>
    </ul>

    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>As the unwitting personification of Death, reality exists to Lily through the veil of a backstage curtain, a transient stage show performed by actors who take their roles only too seriously. But as the Girl-Who-Lived, Lily's role to play is the most important of all, and come hell or high water play it she will, regardless of how awful Wizard Lenin seems to think she is at her job.</p>
    </blockquote>

    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>Harry's tumultuous and sometimes torturous childhood sees him thrown out of the Dursleys. His journey leads him to learn archaic magics, bond with strange creatures, and gain a little sister with a new family. When his past comes looking for him, his return to the Wizarding World will produce ripples in the lives of everyone he touches.</p>
    </blockquote>

  <!--summary-->
    <h6 class="landmark heading">Summary</h6>
    <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
      <p>Harry was never the type to discriminate against his lovers on the basis of supernatural species, it was the 21st Century for Godric's sake! But, unfortunately for Harry, this free way of thinking comes back to bite him in the arse as an impromptu trip to New York with one of his beaus leads to him getting kidnapped by two witches. Carted across the east coast, Harry is dumped on the doorstep, and forced to do the bidding, of one very infamous Hybrid.  Harry had always made it a point to never get involved in anyone else's world-ending affairs, but the town of Mystic Falls and its many characters seem hell-bent on keeping him there. And the longer he stays, the more his own demons come to play. Hopefully, when all is said and done, he'll have something left of himself.</p>
    </blockquote>
